Preliminary Estimates of the Intercensal Population of Counties
1970-1979

Issued April 1982
Source: U.S. Bureau of the Census
        Population Estimates and Population Distribution Branches

Method: The intercensal formula for the 1970s is described in Current
Population Reports, Series P25-957.  The formula was applied to both
state and county estimates.  The intercensal estimates are based on
census counts which include the latest corrections available at the time
of production.  The methodology for the 1970s postcensal estimates is
described in P25-873.
For a copy of these reports call (301) 457-2422.

Note: In 1975 the Federal Government opened camps for Vietnamese
refugees in Sebastion Co., AR, San Diego Co., CA, Dade Co., FL., and
Lebanon Co., PA.  These refugee populations were eventually assimilated
throughout the nation.

State Estimates are rounded to thousands, county estimates are
rounded to hundreds.  Unrounded estimates are not available.

Bor. = Borough,  C.A. = Census Area,  Par. = Parish
